                      <div data-reactid="451">
                       A detached studio with all the amenities needed in a temporary home, it also fuses the two playful worlds of a Swiss Family Robinson-style "treehouse" with a comfy inner-child's dream playhouse... "The Tiny Butterfly House" is located in a quiet neighborhood.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="452">
                       WARNING TALL GUESTS: THE CEILING IS LOW UNDERNEATH THE SLEEPING LOFT, WHERE YOU ENTER THE TINY HOUSE. If you are taller than 5'10", you may not be comfortable staying in this space. Tiny (8’x14’) detached studio in peaceful eco-friendly garden setting. Convenient Topanga location, depending on traffic, 20-30 minutes to Santa Monica or Woodland Hills. Ocean breeze. Views of garden and mountains from spacious deck. Shared bathroom is an inviting stroll to the main house. Choice of indoor or outdoor shower. Amenities include: off street parking, wifi internet, clean towels and sheets, washer &amp; dryer, toaster oven, 2-burner hotplate, pots &amp; pans, eco-friendly soaps: laundry, dish, body, shampoo, and conditioner. Located in quiet neighborhood close to the popular French cafe, Mimosa, a health food store, and other businesses. Limited public transportation.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="453">
                       We love the views of our Canyon and mountains from Valley view Drive. Also, we love the quiet neighborhood, generally very peaceful. We also love that it is a short walk (1/2 mile) to local businesses, such as the very popular Mimosa Cafe.
                      </div>

                       <li data-reactid="471"><p data-reactid="472">Wow, what an amazing place! It's difficult to do it justice in words, but I will give it a try. Andrea's photos give an idea of the setting and the space, but it's really a place that's hard to convey even in photos. I loved the outdoor lifestyle, with the kitchen out on a partly covered verandah, where there's a great view of the canyon and the garden below. It's like cooking in a garden, or even camping/glamping. And the bathroom is just off to the side of the indoor living space, so you don't have to steam up the whole house when you take a shower (like the place I'm staying now. Haha). Also, the outdoor kitchen means that the refrigerator is outside, so you don't have to listen to it revving up all night long, like many small studios I've stayed in. I grew up in a rural area, so I appreciate a quiet space to sleep. The indoor space is indeed tiny, especially for a giant beast like me (6 feet four inches, 190 pounds), but it's very, very functional. In fact, I found the space more functional than many places I've stayed where I had twice or even three times as much space. Andrea seems to have thought about everything that a visitor might want, and placed it in the exact spot where one might expect to find it. Piles of extra comforters and blankets to heap on top of you on a cold night? Check. Ziploc baggies to take a snack for the beach? Check. Pair of scissors to cut out a clothing tag that's itching you? You bet. It's all there. Topanga Canyon is such a special place, as I learned from my two weeks at Andrea's. And this space has been set up to take full advantage of what makes Topanga special, from the slow-burning sunsets to the the quiet, dark nights. It might be a bit out of the ordinary for some people to live partly outdoors like this, but it's a really balanced way to exist. That's what I realized two nights ago, when I got up for a glass of water, and the only sounds I heard from the verandah were the calls of two Great Horned Owls, duetting across Topanga Canyon.                       <div data-reactid="1163">
                       The Subterranean Terrace Room at The Enchanted Cottage offers comfort, beauty, and convenience for travelers on a budget. Within walking distance to the center of town, this self-contained apartment is equipped with everything you need for meal prep
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1164">
                       The Subterranean Terrace room: This private mini-apartment, is nestled into the earth, yet, its entrance overlooks the lower gardens, as well. Picturesque windows look out into the lovely entry garden. From the built-in "day bed" (a reading and relaxing nook), you can watch the birds and butterflies (seasonal) as they flutter about the garden. The room also features a comfortable, medium-firm full-sized bed. In addition, you may organize your clothes on hangers provided, and in dresser drawers. PLEASE BE AWARE: THE TWO BEAMS IN THIS ROOM ARE LOW AND NOT SUITABLE FOR GUESTS OVER 5' 9" (175cm) TALL. The shared outdoor patio areas offer delightful seating for sipping coffee or tea, or dining, while enjoying beautiful views of the garden, and of the nearby mountains and trees. The butterflies, birds, and bees are very happy here in the Gardens of The Enchanted Cottage, and you will be too! Like to eat fresh, organic food? For an added price and a brief orientation, you can have access to the food growing in the gardens.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1165">
                       Valley View is a quiet street in "climate perfect" Fernwood, located just one-half mile from local businesses, including the popular Mimosa Cafe, where locals mingle and visitors plug in... as well as enjoying a delicious cup of coffee! Valley View Drive, a relatively steep climb, provides an excellent workout. Neighbors are friendly, yet keep to themselves. The beach is four miles away. Santa Monica is a 20-30 minute drive. The valley (Woodland Hills) is also a 20-30 minute drive.

                      <div data-reactid="1616">
                       JoyHouse8 is a healing, inspiring, relaxing retreat space convenient to everything. With spectacular views of several layers of mountains, nestled into the side of the Santa Monica mountains, enjoy bird watching and these lovely natural surroundings. The guest room is a cozy space with a luxury queen mattress, plenty of windows and natural light, a full, attached, private bathroom with all the amenities, closet, small desk, and tv with HBO and Showtime (Direct tv, satellite).

                      <div data-reactid="1617">
                       Perfect for anyone looking to get back to nature while staying in touch with the world. OUTSIDE: JoyHouse8 offers spectacular views ideal for birdwatching, nature photography, artist's and writer's retreats or just relaxing on the large view deck and various patios spread around the mountainside property. The views at JoyHouse8 have been called some of the most beautiful in the world! By day, enjoy views of birds bathing at the view deck bird bath and flying over the rolling green Woodland Hills below, several layers of mountains, and the northwestern edge of the San Fernando Valley. A landscape painters dream! At night enjoy the glistening city lights. JoyHouse8 is an amazing place to spend the fourth of July watching the many fireworks displays going on throughout the valley below. INSIDE: elegant, creative decor gives JoyHouse8 a comfortable, cozy, spacious, artist studio vibe. JoyHouse8 was built only five years ago and offers: - one cozy, guest room with deliciously comfortable, luxury, queen mattress and en suite full bathroom. - an office with a flexible space for meetings, treatments, and work - a large great room with spectacular view and separate kitchen, cozy living room, dining area with enormous birchwood table with leaf and many chairs for meetings, workshops, dinner parties. (*Special arrangement and extra fees apply) We also offer JoyHouse8 as a whole house rental, the monthly price listed here reflects that, the single guest room is not currently available for long term stays (three weeks max). The whole house offers 2 bedrooms with 2-1/2 attached bathrooms including a roomie master bedroom with attached full bath with separate shower and soaking tub with big picture window views of the sky, side deck and mountainside garden. The whole house can comfortably fit up to 4 people, with two luxurious queen beds.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1618">
                       Our little neighborhood is friendly, safe and quiet. It is also very convenient for whatever you want to do. The beach is a gorgeous 15 minute drive through historical Topanga Canyon. Topanga Canyon (10 mins through the mountains) is an adorable little mountain town chock full of creative folks, with eclectic cafes, restaurants, galleries, gift shops, hiking, and general mountain exploration and drives. Calabasas is the next town over and just 5 minutes up Mulholland Drive to Old Town Calabasas, shops, and the awesome Saturday morning Farmer's Market. We are also five minutes from the 101, the fabulous new outdoor mall The Village, the Topanga Mall, Whole Foods, Trader Joe's, Sprouts, a myriad of restaurants and cafes &amp; several gyms. LA, Hollywood, Studio City, Santa Monica, Venice Beach: Anywhere into the city is generally about a 45 minute drive (give our take for traffic etc.). Whenever you can we recommend taking the scenic drive through Topanga Canyon and along the ocean on the historic Pacific Coast Highway. If you're flying in the Bob Hope airport in Burbank is recommended.
                      </div>

                      <div data-reactid="1874">
                       Wake up in our beautiful, light-filled modern home nestled in the Santa Monica mountains, surrounded by palm trees and open sky. This family home sleeps 5 and is within easy reach of Santa Monica, LA, and Malibu.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1875">
                       Set in the hills of Topanga Canyon just a few miles up from the beach, come and enjoy this recently renovated, stylish family home. The house features modern kitchen, highspeed internet and Apple TV, laundry, fenced grassy yard, views, children's playroom, and more! You have State Park trails close by and Pine Tree Circle, Topanga's town center is 3 miles down the road. Hiking, horseback riding, surfing, mountain biking, are all within easy reach. A perfect weekend getaway, worlds removed from the hustle &amp; bustle of LA yet easily accessible. 20 minutes to Santa Monica and Malibu, 15 minutes to Calabasas and Woodland Hills.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1876">
                       Topanga is a unique artsy community nestled in the beautiful Santa Monica mountains, but so close to everything a big cosmopolitan city has to offer. Wake up to hummingbirds and ocean breezes, go to sleep at night listening to the sound of coyotes and owls. Enjoy a book in the hammock at sunset or take a hike around the neighborhood. Or drive up the coast and dine at Nobu or any of the fine restaurants the area has to offer.
                      </div>

I loved the outdoor lifestyle, with the kitchen out on a partly covered verandah, where there's a great view of the canyon and the garden below. It's like cooking in a garden, or even camping/glamping. And the bathroom is just off to the side of the indoor living space, so you don't have to steam up the whole house when you take a shower (like the place I'm staying now. Haha). Also, the outdoor kitchen means that the refrigerator is outside, so you don't have to listen to it revving up all night long, like many small studios I've stayed in. I grew up in a rural area, so I appreciate a quiet space to sleep.  The indoor space is indeed tiny, especially for a giant beast like me (6 feet four inches, 190 pounds), but it's very, very functional. In fact, I found the space more functional than many places I've stayed where I had twice or even three times as much space. Andrea seems to have thought about everything that a visitor might want, and placed it in the exact spot where one might expect to find it. Piles of extra comforters and blankets to heap on top of you on a cold night? Check. Ziploc baggies to take a snack for the beach? Check. Pair of scissors to cut out a clothing tag that's itching you? You bet. It's all there.  Topanga Canyon is such a special place, as I learned from my two weeks at Andrea's. And this space has been set up to take full advantage of what makes Topanga special, from the slow-burning sunsets to the the quiet, dark nights.
